# GOOD CORPORATE GOVERNANCE

![](https://cdn-mineru.openxlab.org.cn/result/2025-10-20/11459e92-cf5e-4cf6-b14f-7d2ffea99629/92fc230b252e95f2d0691bdb31bec5449a7dab8a61c89e49e85bc09e59e4818a.jpg)

# KEBIJAKAN DAN STRUKTUR TATA KELOLA PERUSAHAAN

# CORPORATE GOVERNANCE POLICY AND STRUCTURE

# Kebijakan Tata Kelola

Penerapan tata kelola perusahaan yang baik kepada good corporate governance (GCG) merupakan landasan bagi perusahaan untuk menjaga aktivitas bisnis berjalan dengan baik, bertanggung jawab,serta memenuhi ketentuan dan peraturan perundang-undangan yang berlaku. Selain itu, penerapan GCG dilakukan untuk menjaga keberlangsungan usaha dalam jangka panjang dan menjaga nilai kepada pemangku kepentingan.

Dalam upaya mencapkan GCG yang komprehensif dan efektif, Perseroan mencapkan prinsip-prinsip GCG yang telah dikembangkan oleh Komite Nasional Kebijakan Governansi (KNKG) dan diungkapkan pada Pedoman Umum Governansi Corporat Indonesia (PUGKI) 2021. Adapun prinsip-prinsip GCG tersebut diuraikan sebagai berikut.

# Corporate Governance Policy

The implementation of good corporate governance (GCG) is the foundation for companies to maintain business activities running well, responsibly, and comply with applicable laws and regulations. In addition, the implementation of GCG is carried out to maintain business continuity in the long term and maintain value to stakeholders.

In an effort to implement comprehensive and effective GCG, the Company applies GCG principles that have been developed by the National Committee for Government Policy (NCGP) and disclosed in the 2021 Indonesian General Corporate Government Guidelines (IGCGG). The GCG principles are outlined as follows.

![](https://cdn-mineru.openxlab.org.cn/result/2025-10-20/11459e92-cf5e-4cf6-b14f-7d2ffea99629/0a6c718ca2eea97e04a1ceecc696225fc3950b3c70a2f6f3e4e0f0155d241983.jpg)

# Perilaku Beretika Ethical Behavior

Perseroan senantiasa menginedepankan keujuratan, memperlakukan semua pihak dengan hormat (respect), memenuhi komitmen, membrangun serta menjaga nilainilai moral dan kepercayaan secara konsisten. Perseroan juga memperhatikan kepentingan Pemegang Saham dan pemangku kepentingan lainnya berdasarkan asas kewajaran dan kesetaraan (fairness) dan dikelola secara independen Seeingga masing-masing organ Perseroan tidak saling mendominasi dan tidak dapat diintervensi oleh pihak lainnya.

The Company always prioritizes honesty, treats all parties with respect, fulfills commitments, builds and maintains moral values and beliefs consistently. The Company also pays attention to the interests of Shareholders and other stakeholders based on the principles of fairness and is managed independently so that each organ of the Company does not dominate each other and cannot be intervened by other parties.

![](https://cdn-mineru.openxlab.org.cn/result/2025-10-20/11459e92-cf5e-4cf6-b14f-7d2ffea99629/d5d448eeaf4eeeff9f46280e072014746161288dcf86f30db2b9b2456eccb97b.jpg)

# Akuntabilitas Accountability

Perseroan dapat mempertanggungjawabkan kinerjanya secara transparan dan wajar. Untuk itu, Perseroan harus dikelola dengan benar, terukur, dan seksuai dengan kepentingan korporat dengan tetap mempertimbangkan kepentingan Pemegang Saham dan pemangku kepentingan. Akuntabilitas merupakan prasyarat yang diperlukan untuk mencapai kinerja yang berkelanjutan.

The Company can account for its performance transparently and fairly. For this reason, the Company must be managed correctly, measurably, and in accordance with corporate interests while considering the interests of Shareholders and stakeholders. Accountability is a necessary prerequisite for achieving sustainable performance.

![](https://cdn-mineru.openxlab.org.cn/result/2025-10-20/11459e92-cf5e-4cf6-b14f-7d2ffea99629/23165a2000d1764fefaf8205a54e2289b52eecbb60c800145009af27611211e8.jpg)

# Transparansi Transparency

Untuk menjaga obyektivitas dalam menjalankan bisnis, Perseroan menyediakan informasi yang material dan relevant dengan cara yang mudah diakses dan dipahami oleh pemangku kepentingan. Perseroan mengambilinisiatif untuk mengungkapkan tidak hatanya masalah yang disyaratkan oleh peraturan perundang-undangan, tetapi juga hal yang penting untuk pengambilan keputusan oleh Pemegang Saham, kreditur, dan pemangku kepentingan lainnya.

To maintain objectivity in conducting business, the Company provides material and relevant information in a way that is easily accessible and understood by stakeholders. The Company takes the initiative to disclose not only issues hinted by laws and regulations, but also matters that are important for decision making by Shareholders, creditors, and other stakeholders.

![](https://cdn-mineru.openxlab.org.cn/result/2025-10-20/11459e92-cf5e-4cf6-b14f-7d2ffea99629/da5a381bf7be6bcebdfa6b85ad511a7ec8f5b4c1303c9d6b4515801661836e7c.jpg)

# Keberlanjutan Sustainability

Perseroan mematuhi peraturan perundang-undangan dan berkomitmen melaksanan tanggung jawab terhadap masyarakat dan lingkungan,agar berkontribusi pada pembangunan bergelanjutan melalui kerja sama dengan semua pemangku kepentingan erkait untuk mencatingkan kehidupan yang selaras dengan kepentingan bisnis dan agenda pembangunan berkelanjutan.

The Company complies with laws and regulations and is committed to carrying out its responsibility towards society and the environment, in order to contribute to sustainable development through cooperation with all relevant stakeholders to improve lives in line with business interests and the sustainable development agenda.

# Struktur Tata Kelola

Perseroan senantiasa seksajakomitmen untuk menerapkan dan mencatkan GCG yang efektif di lingkungan internal, sudah satunya dengan mementuk struktur GCG Perseroan. Struktur tersebut dibentuk berdasarkan Undang-Undang No. 40tentang Perseroan Terbatas, seda peraturan dan kebikan terkait lainnya. Adapun struktur GCG Perseroan terdiri dari Rapat Umum Pemegang Saham (RUPS), Dewan Komisaris, Direksi, Komite Audit, Sekretaris Perusahaan, seda Unit Audit Internal. Masing-masing organ tersebut menjalankan tugas dan tanggung jawab seksui dengan ketentuan yang berlaku.

# Governance Structure

The Company always maintains its commitment to implement and improve effective GCG in the internal environment, one of which is by establishing the Company's GCG structure. The structure is established based on Law No. 40 on Limited Liability Companies, as well as other related regulations and policies. The Company's GCG structure consists of the General Meeting of Shareholders (GMS), Board of Commissioners, Board of Directors, Audit Committee, Corporate Secretary, and Internal Audit Unit. Each of these organs carries out duties and responsibilities in accordance with applicable regulations.

The implementation of public company governance guidelines refers to Circular Letter No. 32/SEOJK.04/2015, which is outlined as follows.

# RAPAT UMUM PEMEGANG SAHAM

# GENERAL MEETING OF SHAREHOLDERS

Rapat Umum Pemegang Saham (RUPS) merupakan forum teringgi di internal Perseroan yang mempunyai hak dan wewenang untuk menerima pertanggungjawaban dari Dewan Komisaris dan Direksi Perseroan,{serta mengambil keputusan penting erkait aktivitas bisnis. Perseroan melaksanan RUPS berdasarkan Undang-Undang No. 40 tantal Tang Perseroan Terbatas, Anggaran Dasar, dan Peraturan Otoritas Jasa Keuangan No. 15/POJK.04/2020 tantal Tang Rencana dan Penyelenggaraan Rapat Umum Pemegang Saham Perseroan Terbuka.

Perseroan wajib melaksanakan RUPS setiap tahun maksimal setelah 6 bulan tahun buku,{serta dapat melaksanakan RUPS secara insidental seksuai kebutuhan Dewan Komisaris, Direksi, dan Pemegang Saham.

# Pelaksanaan RUPS 2023

Di tahun 2023, Perseroan telah melaksanan RUPS Tahunan pada tanggal 20 Juni 2023 bertempat di The Bellezza Suites Permata Hijau JI. Soepeno No. 34, Permata Hijau Jakarta Selatan. Tahapan pelaksanaan RUPS Tahunan 2023 diungkapkan sebagai berikut.

The General Meeting of Shareholders (GMS) is the highest forum within the Company that has the right and authority to accept accountability from the Company's Board of Commissioners and Board of Directors, as well as make important decisions related to business activities. The Company conducts GMS based on Law No. 40 concerning Limited Liability Companies, Articles of Association, and Financial Services Authority Regulation No. 15/POJK.04/2020 concerning Plan and Implementation of General Meeting of Shareholders of Public Companies.

The Company is required to hold GMS every year maximum after 6 months of the financial year, and can carry out GMS incidentally according to the needs of the Board of Commissioners, Board of Directors, and Shareholders.

# 2023 GMS Implementation

In 2023, the Company has held the Annual GMS on June 20, 2023 at The Bellezza Suites Permata Hijau, JI. Soepeno No. 34, Permata Hijau, South Jakarta. The stages of the 2023 Annual GMS are disclosed as follows.

# Pelaksanaan RUPS Tahunan 2022

Sepanjang tahun 2022, Perseroanbelum漫长ukanan RUPS Tahunan karena telah menjadi perusahaan tertutup dan tidak mempunyai kewajiban untuk melaksananakan RUPS Tahunan tersebut. Namun demikian, untuk mengambil keputusan dari Pemegang Saham, Perseroan漫长ukan Keputusan Sirkuler yang disetujui oleh seluruh Pemegang Saham, Dewan Komisaris, dan Direksi.

# 2022 GMS Implementation

Throughout 2022, the Company has not conducted an Annual GMS because it is still a closed company and has no obligation to carry out the Annual GMS. However, to make decisions from Shareholders, the Company conducts Circular Resolutions approved by all Shareholders, the Board of Commissioners, and the Board of Directors.

# DEWAN KOMISARIS BOARD OF COMMISSIONERS

Dewan Komisaris merupakan organ yang menjalankan tugas danggangungjawab untuk mengawasi pelaksanaan tugas Direksi, sama memberikan masukan dan saran yang objektif dan independen perkait pengurusan dan pengelolaan Perseroan yang dilakukan oleh Direksi.

# Pedoman Kerja

Dewan Komisaris melaksanakan tugas dan tanggung jawab berpedoman pada Anggaran Dasar dan Peraturan Otoritas Jasa Keuangan No. 33/POJK.04/2014tentang Dewan Komisaris dan Direksi Emiten ata Perusahaan Publik.

# Komposisi dan Keanggotaan

Pada tahun 2023, komposisi Dewan Komisaris Perseroan terdiri dari 1 Komisaris Utama dan 1 Komisaris Independen yang diungkapkan sebagai berikut.

The Board of Commissioners is an organ that carries out duties and responsibilities to oversee the implementation of the duties of the Board of Directors, as well as provide objective and independent input and suggestions related to the management and management of the Company carried out by the Board of Directors.

# Work Guidelines

The Board of Commissioners carries out its duties and responsibilities based on the Articles of Association and Financial Services Authority Regulation No. 33/POJK.04/2014 concerning the Board of Commissioners and Directors of Issuers or Public Companies.

# Composition and Membership

In 2023, the composition of the Company's Board of Commissioners consists of 1 President Commissioner and 1 Independent Commissioner which is disclosed as follows.

# Komisaris Independen

Komisaris Independen merupakan pihak eksternal Perseroan yang ditunjuk berdasarkan kriteria Komisaris Independen yang berlaku dan sesuai dengan Peraturan Otoritas Jasa Keuangan No. 33/POJK.04/2014 tersebut Dewan Komisaris dan Direksi Perusahaan Publik atas Emiten,serta telah memenuhi kriteria sebagai berikut.

1. Berasal dari luar perusahaan publik.  
2. Tidak mempunyai hubungan afliasi dengan Perseroan, Dewan Komisaris, Direksi dan/atau Pemegang Saham Utama perusahaan.  
3. Tidak memiliki hubungan usaha, baik langsung maupun tidak langsung, berkaitan dengan usaha Perseroan.  
4. Tidak memiliki saham, baik langsung maupun tidak langsung di Perseroan.  
5. Tidak bekerja rangkap sebagai Direktur di perusahaan lainnya yang terafiliasi dengan Perseroan.  
6. Dapat memahami peraturan perundang-undangan di bidang pasar modal.

Di tahun 2023, Perseroan telah menunjuk 1 orang yang menjadi sebagai Komisaris Independen, yaitu Bapak Hadi Avilla Tamzil. Beliau telah memenuhi kriteria dan ketentuan yang berlaku sebagai Komisaris Independen.

# Independent Commissioner

Independent Commissioner is an external party of the Company appointed based on the applicable criteria of Independent Commissioner and in accordance with the Financial Services Authority Regulation No. 33/POJK.04/2014 concerning the Board of Commissioners and Directors of Public Companies or Issuers, and has met the following criteria.

1. Comes from outside the public company.  
2. Has no affiliation with the Company, Board of Commissioners, Board of Directors and/or Major Shareholder of the company.  
3. Does not have a business relationship, either directly or indirectly, related to the Company's business.  
4. Does not own shares, either directly or indirectly in the Company.  
5. Does not work concurrently as Director in other companies affiliated with the Company.  
6. Able to understand laws and regulations in the field of capital markets.

In 2023, the Company has appointed 1 person who serves as an Independent Commissioner, who is Mr. Hadi Avilla Tamzil. He has fulfilled the applicable criteria and conditions as an Independent Commissioner.

# Independensi

Seluruh Dewan Komisaris mencutamakan independensinya, integritas, dan objektivitas dalam melaksanan peran, tugas,serta tanggung jawabnya. Komitmen ini ditunjukkan dengan tidak adanya hubungan afliasi, baik keuangan ataupun kekeluargaan antar anggota Dewan Komisaris lainnya, anggota Direksi, ataupun Pemegang Saham.

# Tugas dan Tanggung Jawab

Dewan Komisaris menjalankan tugas dan tanggung jawab berpedoman pada peraturan yang berlakuserta Anggaran Dasar Perseroan,segagai berikut.

a. Melakukan pengawasan dan bertanggungjawab atas pengawasan terhadap kebijingan pengurusan, jalannya pengurusan pada umumnya, baik mengenai Perseroan maupun usaha Perseroan, dan memberi nasihat kepada Direksi.  
b. Memberikan persetujuan atas rencana kerja tahunan Perseroan, selambat-lambatnya sebelum dimulainya tahun buku yang akan datang.  
c. Melakukan tugas yang secara khusus diberikan kepadanya menurut Anggaran Dasar, peraturan perundang-undangan yang berlaku dan/atau berdasarkan keputusan RUPS.  
d. Melakukan tugas, wewenang, dan tanggung jawab seksuai dengan ketentuan Anggaran Dasar Perseroan dan keputusan RUPS.  
e. Meneliti dan menelaah laporan tahun yang dispersiapkan oleh Direksianya menandatangani Laporan Tahunan tersebut.  
f. Mematuhi Anggaran Dasar dan peraturan perundangundangan, serta wajib melaksanan prinsip-prinsip profesalisme, efisiensi, transparansi, kemandirian, akuntabilitas, pertanggungjawaban, serta kewajaran.  
g. Melaksanakan fungsi nominasi dan remunerasi sesuai dengan ketentuan dan peraturan perundangan yang berlaku.  
h. Mengawasi pelaksanaan rencana kerja tanunan Perseroan.  
i. Mengikuti perkembangan kegiatan Perseroan, dan dalam hal Perseroan menunjukkan gezala kemunduran yang mencolok, segera melaporkan kepada RUPS dengan disertai saran mengenai langkah perbaikan yang harus ditempuh.  
j. Memberikan pendapat dan saran kepada RUPS mengenai setiap persoalan lainnya yang dianggap penting bagi pengelolaan Perseroan.  
k. Melakukan tugas pengawasan lainnya yang ditentukan oleh RUPS.  
I. Memberikan tanggapan atas laporan berkala Direksi dan pada setiap waktu yang diperlukan mengenai perkembangan Perseroan.

# Tugas dan Tanggung Jawab Komisaris Utama

Di samping menjalankan tugas secara umum, Komisaris Utama mempunyai tugas inti, yaitu memberikan arahan kepada anggota Dewan Komisaris, memimpin rapat internal dan gabungan Dewan Komisaris dan Direksi,{serta memimpin pelaksanaan RUPS Tahunan ataupun RUPS Luar Biasa.

# Independency

The Board of Commissioners prioritizes independency, integrity, and objectivity in carrying out their roles, duties, and responsibilities. This commitment is shown by the absence of affiliation, financial or familial relationships between other members of the Board of Commissioners, members of the Board of Directors, or Shareholders.

# Duties and Responsibilities

The Board of Commissioners carries out its duties and responsibilities based on the applicable regulations and the Company's Articles of Association, as follows.

a. supervise and be responsible for supervising management policies, the general management of both the Company and the Company's business, and provide advice to the Board of Directors.  
b. Give approval for the Company's annual work plan, not later than before the start of the next financial year.  
c. Carry out tasks specifically assigned to him according to the Articles of Association, applicable laws and regulations and/or based on GMS decisions.  
d. Carry out duties, authorities and responsibilities in accordance with the provisions of the Company's Articles of Association and the resolutions of the GMS.  
e. Research and review the annual report prepared by the Board of Directors and sign the Annual Report.  
f. Comply with the Articles of Association and laws and regulations, and must implement the principles of professionalism, efficiency, transparency, independence, accountability, responsibility and fairness.  
g. Carry out the nomination and remuneration functions in accordance with the applicable laws and regulations.  
h. Supervise the implementation of the Company's annual work plan.  
i. Following the development of the Company's activities, and in the event that the Company shows striking symptoms of decline, immediately report to the GMS accompanied by suggestions regarding corrective steps that must be taken.  
j. Provide opinions and suggestions to the GMS regarding any other issues deemed important for the management of the Company.  
k. Carry out other supervisory duties determined by the GMS.  
I. Provide responses to the periodic reports of the Board of Directors and at any time necessary regarding the development of the Company.

# Duties and Responsibilities of President Commissioner

In addition to carrying out general duties, the President Commissioner has the core duties, which are providing direction to members of the Board of Commissioners, chairing internal and joint meetings of the Board of Commissioners and Board of Directors, and presiding over the implementation of the Annual GMS or Extraordinary GMS.

# Keputusan yang Memerlukan Persetujuan Dewan Komisaris

Selain meldawasi kinerja Direksi, Dewan Komisaris mempunyai hak khusus dalam meld Gambil keputusan, di antaranya pemindahan kekayaan Perseroan ata menjadikan jaminan utang kekayaan Perseroan, persetujuan transaksi meminjam ata meminjamkan uang, serta persetujuan untuk mendirikan suatu usaha bara ata turut serta pada perusahaan lain.

# Pelaksanaan Tugas

Dewan Komisaris telah seksukan peran, tugas dan tanggung jawab sesuai dengan pedoman kerja yang berlaku, yang diuraikan sebagai berikut.

1. Mengawasi pelaksanaan tugas dan tanggung jawab Direksi secara keseluruhan.  
2. Memberikan saran, nasihat, serta rekomendasi sesuai dengan kebjakan dan strategi yang dibutuhkan oleh Direksi.  
3. Menyampaikan Laporan Pengawasan Dewan Komisaris dalam RUPS Tahunan.  
4. Melakukan rapat internal Dewan Komisaris sebanyak 4 kali, serta rapat gabungan bersama Direksi sebanyak 4 kali pada tahun 2023.  
5. Melakukan rapat gabungan dengan Komite Audit.  
6. Melakukan evaluasi atas audit Laporan Keuangan yang dilakukan oleh kantor akuntan publik tahun buku 2022 dan menujuk akuntan publik/kantor akuntan publik atas rekomendasi Komite Audit.

# Rapat

Pelaksanaan rapat internal Dewan Komisaris paling sedikit dilakukan 1 kali dalam 3 bulan,<sertaRAPAT gabungan dengan Direksi minimal 1 kali dalam 4 bulan.Pada tahun 2023,Dewan Komisaris telah melaksanan rapat internal sebanyak 4 kali dan rapat gabungan Dewan Komisaris dan Direksi sebanyak 4 kali, yang diuraikan sebagai berikut.

# Decisions Requiring Board of Commissioners Approval

In addition to supervising the performance of the Board of Directors, the Board of Commissioners has special rights in making decisions, including transferring the Company's assets or making debt guarantees for the Company's assets, approving transactions to borrow or lend money, and approving to establish a new business or participate in other companies.

# Implementation of Duties

The Board of Commissioners has performed its roles, duties and responsibilities in accordance with the applicable work guidelines, which are outlined as follows.

1. Supervise the implementation of duties and responsibilities of the Board of Directors as a whole.  
2. Provide advice, advice, and recommendations in accordance with policies and strategies required by the Board of Directors.  
3. Submit the Supervisory Report of the Board of Commissioners at the Annual GMS.  
4. Conducting internal meetings of the Board of Commissioners as many as 4 times, as well as joint meetings with the Board of Directors as many as 4 times in 2023.  
5. Conduct joint meetings with the Audit Committee.  
6. Evaluate the Financial Statement audit conducted by a public accounting firm for the 2022 financial year and appoint a public accountant/public accounting firm on the recommendation of the Audit Committee.

# Meeting

Internal meetings of the Board of Commissioners are held at least 1 time in 4 months, and joint meetings with the Board of Directors at least 1 time in 4 months. In 2023, the Board of Commissioners has conducted internal meetings as many as 4 times and joint meetings of the Board of Commissioners and Board of Directors as many as 4 times, which are outlined as follows.

# Pengembangan Kompetensi

Dewan Komisaris melaksanakan kegiatan pengembangan kompetensi dalam upaya memperlugas pemaham dan wawasan terkait aktivitas bisnis yang difalankan dan memaksimalkan pelaksanaan tugas. Sepanjang tahun 2023, Dewan Komisaris telah mengikuti kegiatan pengembangan kompetensi sebagai berikut.

# Competency Development

The Board of Commissioners carries out competency development activities in an effort to broaden understanding and insight related to business activities carried out and maximize the implementation of duties. Throughout 2023, the Board of Commissioners has participated in the following competency development activities.

# Penilaian Kinerja Dewan Komisaris

Secara berkala Perseroan mencevaluasi kinerja anggota Dewan Komisaris, baik secara bersama-sama ataupun per individu. Penilaian tersebut dilakukan melalui pelaksanaan RUPS Tahunan, yaitu dalam Penyampaian Laporan Pengawasan, serta pelaksanaan penilaian sendiri (self-assessment) oleh masing-masing anggota Dewan Komisaris sesuai dengan kriteria yang telah ditetapkan. Kriteria penilaian kinerja Dewan Komisaris Perseroan, di antaranya: pelaksanaan rapat internal dan gabungan dengan Direksi, kehadiran dan participasi dalam rapat, kontribusi pengawasan, serta kualitas dan intensitas pemberian saran kepada Direksi.

Pada tahun 2023, Dewan Komisaris telah makukanan tugas dan tanggung jawab dengan baik, seksuai dengan pedoman kerja yang berlaku dan tidak melewati batas ketentuan yang telah ditetapkan. Selain itu, Dewan Komisaris berkontribusi aktif dalam mengawasi ataupun memberikan saran, nasihat, seda rekomendasi kepada Direksi.

# Penilaian Kinerja Komite Audit

Penilaian kinerja Komite Audit dilakukan secara berkala untuk mencevaluasi pencapaian pelaksanaan tugas dan target yang ditetapkan. Penilaian tersebut dilakukan berdasarkan kriteria yang telah ditetapkan, di antaranya: efektivitas pelaksanaan tugas dan tanggung jawab, kehadiran dan keaktifan rapat,{serta rekomendasi dan saran kepada Dewan Komisaris.

Sepanjang tahun 2023, Komite Audit telah seksukan tugas dan tanggung jawab dengan baik, yang dapat dilihat dari pelaksanaan audit dan analisis Laporan Keuangan Perseroan, rekomendasi penunjukan akuntan publik, seda pengawasan terhadap systemd pengendalian internal danSYSTEM manajemen risiko.

# Performance Assessment of the Board of Commissioners

Periodically, the Company evaluates the performance of members of the Board of Commissioners, either jointly or individually. The assessment is carried out through the implementation of the Annual GMS, which are in the Submission of Supervisory Reports, as well as the implementation of self-assessment by each member of the Board of Commissioners in accordance with predetermined criteria. Performance assessment criteria of the Company's Board of Commissioners, including: implementation of internal and joint meetings with the Directors, attendance and participation in meetings, supervisory contributions, and the quality and intensity of providing advice to the Directors.

In 2023, the Board of Commissioners has performed its duties and responsibilities properly, in accordance with the applicable work guidelines and has not exceeded the limits of the stipulated provisions. In addition, the Board of Commissioners actively contributes in supervising or providing advice, advice, and recommendations to the Directors.

# Audit Committee Performance Assessment

The Audit Committee's performance appraisal is carried out periodically to evaluate the achievement of the implementation of the tasks and targets set. The assessment is carried out based on predetermined criteria, including: the effectiveness of the implementation of duties and responsibilities, attendance and activeness of meetings, as well as recommendations and suggestions to the Board of Commissioners.

Throughout 2023, the Audit Committee has carried out its duties and responsibilities well, which can be seen from the audit and analysis of the Company's Financial Statements, recommendations for the appointment of public accountants, as well as supervision of the internal control system and risk management system.

# DIREKSI

# BOARD OF DIRECTORS

Direksi merupakan organ Perseroan yang bertugas untuk mengatur, mengelola, dan mengurus seluruh aktivitas operasional dan keuangan, termasuk mencapai Visi, Misi, dan target yang telah ditetapkan oleh Pemegang Saham ataupun Anggaran Dasar. Direksi harus bertindak denganPTHenh kehati-hatian, waspada, dan senantiasa berada dalam koridor kepadahan.

# Pedoman Kerja

Pelaksanaan tugas Direksi berpedoman pada Anggaran Dasar dan Peraturan Otoritas Jasa Keuangan No. 33/POJK.04/2014 tersebut Dewan Komisaris dan Direksi Emiten ata Perusahaan Publik. Pedoman kerja tersebut sebagai panduan bagi Direksi dalam menjalankan wewenang, serta tugas dan tanggung jawab.

# Komposisi dan Keanggotaan

Pada tahun 2023, komposisi dan keanggotaan Direksi Perseroan terdiri dari 1 Direktur Utama dan 3 Direktur yang diungkapkan sebagai berikut.

The Board of Directors is the Company's organ tasked with regulating, managing, and managing all operational and financial activities, including achieving the Vision, Mission, and targets set by the Shareholders or the Articles of Association. The Board of Directors must act with prudence, vigilance, and always stay within the corridor of compliance.

# Work Guidelines

The implementation of the duties of the Board of Directors is guided by the Articles of Association and Regulation of the Financial Services Authority No. 33/POJK.04/2014 concerning the Board of Commissioners and Directors of Issuers or Public Companies. The work guidelines serve as a guide for the Board of Directors in exercising their authority, duties and responsibilities.

# Composition and Membership

In 2023, the composition and membership of the Board of Directors of the Company consist of 1 President Director and 3 Directors which are disclosed as follows.

# Tugas dan Tanggung Jawab

Direksi menjalankan tugas, tanggung jawab, dan wewenang berpedoman pada peraturan yang berlakuserta Anggaran Dasar Perseroan, sebagai berikut.

# Tugas

a. Direksi bertugas menjalankan dan bertanggung jawab atas pengurusan Emiten kepada Perusahaan Publik untuk kepentingan Emiten kepada Perusahaan Publik sesuai dengan maksud dan tujuan Emiten kepada Perusahaan Publik yang ditetapkan dalam Anggaran Dasar.  
b. Dalam menjalankan tugas dan tanggung jawab atas pengurusan sebagaiimana dimaksud pada ayat (1), Direksi wajib menjadi enggaraman RUPS tahunan dan RUPS lainnya sebagaimana diatur dalam peraturan perdang-undangan dan Anggaran Dasar.

# Duties and Responsibilities

The Board of Directors carries out duties, responsibilities, and authorities based on applicable regulations and the Company's Articles of Association, as follows.

# Duties

a. The Board of Directors is in charge of carrying out and being responsible for the management of the Issuer or Public Company for the benefit of the Issuer or Public Company in accordance with the aims and objectives of the Issuer or Public Company stipulated in the articles of association.  
b. In carrying out the duties and responsibilities for management as referred to in paragraph (1), the Board of Directors is obliged to hold annual GMS and other GMS as regulated in laws and regulations and Articles of Association.

2023 Performance Highlights

Management Reports

Company Profile

Management Review And Analysis

Good Corporate Governance

Sustainability Report

c. Setiap anggota Direksi wajib melaksanan tugas dan tanggung jawab sebagai dimaksud pada ayat (1) dengan itikad baik, penuh tanggung jawab, dan kehatihan.  
d. Dalam rangka mendukung efektivitas pelaksanaan tugas dan tanggung jawab sebagaimana dimaksud pada ayat (1) Direksi dapat mementuk komite.  
e. Dalam hal dibentuk komite seksagaimana dimaksud pada ayat (4), Direksi wajib melakukan evaluasi terhadap kinerja komite setiap akhir tahun buku.

# Tanggung Jawab

1) Setiap anggota Direksi bertanggung jawab secara tanggung renteng atas kerugian Emiten oleh Perusahaan Publik yang disebabkan oleh kesalahan oleh kelalaian anggota Direksi dalam menjalankan tugasnya.  
2) Anggota Direksi tidak dapat dipertanggungjawabkan atas kerugian Emiten kepada Perusahaan Publik sebagai bagaimana dimaksud pada ayat (1) apabila dapat membuktikan:

a. Kerugian tersebut but bukan karena kesalahan ata kalalaiannya;  
b. Telah melakukan pengurusan dengan itikad baik, penuh tanggung jawab, dan kehati-hatian untuk kepentingan dan sesuai dengan maksud dan tujuan Emiten kepada Perusahaan Publik;  
c. Tidak mempunyai benturan kepentingan baik langsung maupun tidak langsung atas tindakan pengurusan yang mengakibatkan kerugian; dan  
d. Telah mencambil tindakan untuk mencegah timbul atau berlanjutnya kerugian tersebut.

# Wewenang

1) Direksi berwenang menjalankan pengurusan sebagai dimaksud dalam Pasal 12 sesuai dengan kebjikan yang dipandang kepada, sesuai dengan maksud dan tujuan yang ditetapkan dalam Anggaran Dasar.  
2) Direksi berwenang mewakili Emiten atas Perusahaan Publik di dalam dan di luar pengadilan.  
3) Anggota Direksi tidak berwenang mewakili Emiten ata Perusahaan Publik apabila:

a. Terdapat perkara di pengadilan antara Emiten atau Perusahaan Publik dengan anggota Direksi yang bersangkutan; dan  
b. Anggota Direksi yang bersangkutan mempunyai kepentinganyang berbenturan dengan kepada Emiten pada Perusahaan Publik.

4) Dalam hal terdapat keadaan seksagaimana dimaksud pada ayat (2), yang berhak mewakili Emiten kepada Perusahaan Publik adalah:

a. Anggota Direksi lainnya yang tidak mempunyai benturan kepentingan dengan Emiten pada Perusahaan Publik;  
b. Dewan Komisaris dalam hal seluruh anggota Direksi mempunyai benturan kepentingan dengan Emiten kepada Perusahaan Publik; oleh

c. Each member of the Board of Directors must carry out the duties and responsibilities as referred to in paragraph (1) in good faith, full responsibility and prudence.  
d. In order to support the effectiveness of the implementation of duties and responsibilities as referred to in paragraph (1) the Board of Directors may form a committee.  
e. In the event that a committee is formed as referred to in paragraph (4), the Board of Directors is required to evaluate the performance of the committee at the end of each financial year.

# Responsibilities

1) Each member of the Board of Directors is jointly and severally responsible for the loss of the Issuer or Public Company caused by the mistakes or negligence of members of the Board of Directors in carrying out their duties.  
2) Members of the Board of Directors cannot be held responsible for the losses of the Issuer or Public Company as referred to in paragraph (1) if they can prove:

a. The loss is not due to his fault or negligence;  
b. Has carried out the management in good faith, full of responsibility and prudence for the benefit and in accordance with the aims and objectives of the Issuer or Public Company;  
c. Does not have a conflict of interest, either directly or indirectly, for management actions that result in losses; and  
d. Have taken action to prevent the loss from arising or continuing.

# Authorities

1) The Board of Directors has the authority to carry out the management as referred to in Article 12 in accordance with the policies deemed appropriate, in accordance with the aims and objectives set out in the Articles of Association.  
2) The Board of Directors has the authority to represent the Issuer or Public Company in and out of court.  
3) Members of the Board of Directors are not authorized to represent Issuers or Public Companies if:

a. There is a case in court between the Issuer or Public Company and the member of the Board of Directors concerned; and  
b. The member of the Board of Directors concerned has interests that conflict with the interests of the Issuer or Public Company.

4) In the event that there is a situation as referred to in paragraph (2), those who have the right to represent the Issuer or Public Company are:

a. Other members of the Board of Directors who do not have a conflict of interest with the Issuer or Public Company;  
b. The Board of Commissioners in the event that all members of the Board of Directors have a conflict of interest with an Issuer or Public Company; or

c. Pihak lain yang ditunjuk oleh RUPS dalam hal seluruh anggota Direksi kepada Dewan Komisaris mempunyai benturan kepentingan dengan Emiten kepada Perusahaan Publik.

# Pelaksanaan Tugas

Direksi telah melakukan peran, tugas dan tanggung jawab seksuai dengan pedoman kerja yang berlaku, yang diuraikan sebagai berikut.

1. Melaporkan Pengelolaan dan Pengurusan Perseroan kepada Pemegang Saham di dalam pelaksanaan RUPS.  
2. Melaksanakan RUPS Tahunan dan Paparan Publik pada tanggal 20 Juni 2023.  
3. Melakukan penyusunan kebikan dan strategi bisnis Perseroan, termasuk rencana jangka pendek, mengah, dan panjang.  
4. Melakukan evaluasi kinerja organ pendukung, yaitu Sekretaris Perusahaan dan Unit Audit Internal.  
5. Mengikuti rapat gabungan bersama Dewan Komisaris atau dengan Sekretaris Perusahaan dan Unit Audit Internal.

# Rapat

Pelaksanaan rapat internal Direksi paling sedikit dilakukan 1 kali dalam setiap bulan,uminium rapat gabungan dengan Dewan Komisaris minimal 1 kali dalam 3 bulan. Sepanjang tahun 2023, Direksi telah melaksanan rapat internal seabanyak 4 kali dan rapat gabungan sebanyak 16 kali, yang diuraikan sebagai berikut.

c. Other parties appointed by the GMS in the event that all members of the Board of Directors or Board of Commissioners have a conflict of interest with the Issuer or Public Company.

# Implementation of Duties

The Board of Directors has performed roles, duties and responsibilities in accordance with the applicable work guidelines, which are outlined as follows.

1. Reporting the Management and Management of the Company to Shareholders in the implementation of the GMS.  
2. Holding the Annual GMS and Public Expose on June 20, 2023.  
3. Formulate the Company's business policies and strategies, including short, medium and long term plans.  
4. Evaluate the performance of supporting organs, namely the Corporate Secretary and Internal Audit Unit.  
5. Attend joint meetings with the Board of Commissioners or with the Corporate Secretary and Internal Audit Unit.

# Meeting

Internal meetings of the Board of Directors are held at least 1 time every month, and joint meetings with the Board of Commissioners at least 1 time in 3 months. Throughout 2023, the Board of Directors has conducted 4 times and joint meetings as many as 16 times, which are outlined as follows.

# Penilaian Kinerja Direksi

Secara berkala Perseroan mangevaluasi kinerja anggota Direksi melalui penyampaian Laporan Pengelolaan dan Pengurusan Perseroan, ada pelaksanaan penilaian sendiri (self-assessment) oleh masing-masing anggota Direksi sesuai dengan kriteria yang telah ditetapkan. Kriteria penilaian kinerja Direksi Perseroan, di antaranya: pelaksanaan rapat internal dan gabungan dengan Dewan Komisaris, kehadiran dan participasi dalam rapat,enetapan kebjikan dan strategi, serta kualitas dan intensitas pemberian saran kepada Direksi.

Pada tahun 2023, Direksi telah menjadi tugas dan tanggungjawabdenganbaik,sesuai dengan pedoman kerja yang berlaku dan tidak melewati batas ketentuan yang tetah ditetapkan.Selain itu, direksi telah menerapkan kebjakan dan strategi yang kepada dan efektif dalam memaksimalkan kinerja Perseroan.

# Penilaian Organ Pendukung Direksi

Penilaian Kinerja Sekretaris Perusahaan dan Unit Audit Internal dilakukan secara berkala oleh Direksi merujuk pada pedoman kerja yang berlaku, di antaranya efektivitas pelaksanaan tugas dan tanggung jawab, kehadiran dan keaktifan rapat, pencapaian target, serta rekomendasi dan saran kepada Direksi. Sekretaris Perusahaan dan Unit Audit Internal telah melaksanan tugas dan tanggung jawab dengan baik, efektif, dan seksuai pedoman kerja yang berlaku Selama tahun 2023.

# Performance Appraisal of Board of Directors

Periodically, the Company evaluates the performance of members of Directors through the submission of the Company's Management and Management Report, as well as the implementation of self-assessment by each member of the Directors in accordance with predetermined criteria. The criteria for evaluating the performance of Directors of the Company, including: implementation of internal and joint meetings with the Board of Commissioners, attendance and participation in meetings, determination of policies and strategies, and quality and intensity of providing advice to the Directors.

In 2023, the Directors has performed its duties and responsibilities well, in accordance with the applicable work guidelines and has not exceeded the limits of the stipulated provisions. In addition, the Directors has implemented appropriate and effective policies and strategies in maximizing the Company's performance.

# Assessment of Supporting Organs of the Board of Directors

Performance Assessment of the Corporate Secretary and Internal Audit Unit is carried out periodically by the Board of Directors referring to the applicable work guidelines, including effectiveness of the implementation of duties and responsibilities, attendance and activeness of meetings, achievement of targets, as well as recommendations and suggestions to the Board of Directors. The Corporate Secretary and Internal Audit Unit have carried out their duties and responsibilities properly, effectively, and in accordance with the applicable work guidelines during 2023.

# ASPEK PENTING TERKAIT DEWAN KOMISARIS DAN DIREKSI
IMPORTANT ASPECTS RELATED TO THE BOARD OF COMMISSIONERS AND BOARD OF DIRECTORS

# Kebijakan Remunerasi Dewan Komisaris dan Direksi

Perseroan menetapkan kebijakan remunerasi Dewan Komisaris dan Direksi sesuai dengan Anggaran Dasar dan peraturan perdang-undangan yang berlaku. Selain itu, Perseroan memperhatikan usulan dan rekomendasi dari Dewan Komisaris, Pemegang Saham, kondisi keuangan Perseroan, modal kerja, serta kondisi ekonomi, ataupun membrandingkan dengan kebijakan remunerasi di industri sejenis.

Perseroan telah membayarkan remunerasi Dewan Komisaris dan Direksi sebesar Rp300 juta di tahun 2023, mencapat dibandingkan tahun 2022 yang tercatat sebesar Rp250 juta. Remunerasi yang dibayarkan tersebut termasuk gaji pokok dan tunjangan lainnya.

# Kebijakan Nominasi Dewan Komisaris dan Direksi

Dalamupayamempertahankanregenerasikegemimpinan, PerseroanmelaluiKomiteNominasi danRemunerasi makukananbebijakan nominasi atapengusulan untuk calon anggota Dewan Komisaris dan Direksi yang bara. Proses untuk makukanan nominasi tersebut diuraikan sebagai berikut.

1. Komite Nominasi dan Remunerasi mengusulkanNama calon anggota Dewan Komisaris dan Direksi kepada Pemegang Saham dan Direksi.  
2. Apabila name-name yang diusulkan telah disetujui,.make Komite Nominasi dan Remunerasi berwenang memanggil calon tersebut untuk makukanan prosedur pemilihan dan berbagai的前提下 lainnya, termasuk wawancara jika dibutuhkan. Calon-calon terpilih merupakan calon yang memenuhi kriteria Perseroan.  
3. Calon anggota Dewan Komisaris dan anggota Direksi yang terpilih harus mengikuti uji kepada tan dan kelayakan  
4. Calon anggota Dewan Komisaris dan anggota Direksi yang terpilih disahkan dan ditetapkan dalam pelaksanaan RUPS Tahunan.

Di tahun 2023, tidak terjadi perubahan oleh penambahan anggota Dewan Komisaris dan Direksi. Maka dari itu, tidak terdapat kebjikan nominasi yang dilakukan oleh Komite Nominasi dan Remunerasi.

# Program Orientasi Dewan Komisaris dan Direksi yang Baru

Perseroan tidak makukanan program orientasi, baik kepada anggota Dewan Komisaris ataupun Direksi yangbaru Selama tahun 2023. Karena tidak terjadinya perubahan ataupenambahan anggota Dewan Komisaris dan Direksi.

# Remuneration Policy of the Board of Commissioners and Directors

The Company establishes the remuneration policy of the Board of Commissioners and Board of Directors in accordance with the Articles of Association and applicable laws and regulations. In addition, the Company pays attention to proposals and recommendations from the Board of Commissioners, Shareholders, the Company's financial condition, working capital, and economic conditions, or compares with remuneration policies in similar industries.

The Company has paid remuneration to the Board of Commissioners and Directors of Rp300 million in 2023, an increase compared to 2022 which was recorded at Rp250 million. The remuneration paid includes basic salary and other allowances.

# Nomination Policy of the Board of Commissioners and Directors

In an effort to maintain leadership regeneration, the Company through the Nomination and Remuneration Committee conducts a nomination or proposal policy for new candidates for members of the Board of Commissioners and Board of Directors. The process for making such nominations is outlined as follows.

1. The Nomination and Remuneration Committee proposes the names of prospective members of the Board of Commissioners and Directors to the Shareholders and Board of Directors.  
2. If the proposed names have been approved, the Nomination and Remuneration Committee has the authority to summon the candidate to conduct selection procedures and various other stages, including interviews if needed. The selected candidates are candidates who meet the Company's criteria.  
3. Candidates for members of the Board of Commissioners and elected members of the Board of Directors must take the appropriateness and feasibility test.  
4. Candidates for members of the Board of Commissioners and elected members of the Board of Directors are ratified and determined in the implementation of the Annual GMS.

In 2023, there will be no changes or additions to the members of the Board of Commissioners and Directors. Therefore, there is no nomination policy carried out by the Nomination and Remuneration Committee.

# New Board of Commissioners and Directors Orientation Program

The Company does not conduct an orientation program, either to new members of the Board of Commissioners or Directors during 2023. Because there are no changes or additions to members of the Board of Commissioners and Board of Directors.

# KOMITE AUDIT

# AUDIT COMMITTEE

Dalam rangka:Mengeftekifkan pelaksanaan tugas dan tanggung, Dewan Komisaris membrutuk Komite Audit, yang bertugas untuk makukan audit terhadap Laporan Keuangan Perseroan secara Berkala, mengawasi;penerapan systemd pengendalian internal,SYSTEM manajemen risiko,erta pengawasan;penerapan GCG secara komprehensif.

# Pedoman Kerja

Komite Audit melaksanan tugas dan tanggung jawabnya berpedoman pada Peraturan Otoritas Jasa Keuangan No. 55/POJK.04/2015tentang Pembentukan dan Pedoman Pelaksanaan Kerja Komite Audit.

# Komposisi dan Keanggotaan

Komposisi dan keanggotaan Komite Audit per Desember 2023 terdiri dari 1 ketua yang dijabat oleh Komisaris Independen dan 2 orang anggota yang berasal dari pihak eksternal, yang diungkapkan pada tabel berikut.

In order to streamline the implementation of duties and responsibilities, the Board of Commissioners established an Audit Committee, which is tasked with conducting periodic audits of the Company's Financial Statements, supervising the implementation of internal control systems, risk management systems, and comprehensive supervision of GCG implementation.

# Composition and Membership

The composition and membership of the Audit Committee as of December 2023 consists of 1 chairman held by an Independent Commissioner and 2 members from external parties, as disclosed in the following table.

# Composition and Membership

# Independensi

Seluruh anggota Komite Audit(OP) mengutamakan independensinya, integritas, dan objektivitas dalam melaksanan peran, tugas, serta tanggung jawabnya. Selain itu, Komite Audit menghindari adanya intervensi dan benturan kepentingan di internal perusahaan.

# Tugas dan Tanggung Jawab

Komite Audit menjalankan tugas dan tanggung jawab berpedoman pada peraturan yang berlakuserta Anggaran Dasar Perseroan,segagai berikut.

1. Melakukan penelaahan atas informasi keuangan yang akan dikeluarkan Perseroan kepada publik dan/atau pihak otoritas, antara lain Laporan Keuangan, projeksi dan laporan lainnya terkait dengan informasi keuangan Perseroan, termasuk kepada terhadap standar dan kebjikan akuntansi dalam proses penyusunannya.  
2. Melakukan penelaahan atas ketaatan terhadap peraturan perundang-undangan yang berhubungan dengan kegiatan Perseroan.  
3. Memberikan pendapat independen dalam hal terjadi perbedaan pendapat antara manajemen dan akuntan eksternal atas jasa yang diferikannya.  
4. Memberikan rekomendasi kepada Dewan Komisaris mengenai penunjukkan akuntan yang didasarkan pada independensi, ruang lingkup penugasan dan imbalan jasa.  
5. Mendorong terbentuknya systemd pengendalian internal yang memadai dalam pengelolaan perusahaan dengan makukan evaluasi dan memberikan rekomendasi mengenai penyempurnaan systemd pengendalian internal perusahaan dan implementasinya.  
6. Melakukan penelaahan atas pelaksanaan pemeriksaan oleh auditor internal dan mengawasi pelaksanaan tindak lanjut oleh Direksi atas temuan auditor internal.  
7. Melakukan penelaahan terhadap aktivitas pelaksanaan systemd manajemen risiko yang dilakukan oleh Direksi.  
8. Menelaah pengaduan yang Berkaitan dengan proses akuntansi dan pelaporan keuangan Perseroan.  
9. Menelaah independensi dan objektivitas akuntan publik.  
10. Melakukan penelaahan atas kecukupan pemeriksuan yang dilakukan oleh akuntan publik.  
11. Melakukan pemeriksaan terhadap dugaan adanya kesalahan dalam keputusan rapat Direksi ata gunyimpangan dalam pelaksanaan telah keputusan rapat Direksi.  
12. Menyampaikan laporan tersebut penelaahan kepada seluruh anggota Dewan Komisaris Perseroan setelah selesainya laporan tersebut penelaahan yang dilakukan oleh Komite Audit.  
13. Menelaah dan memberikan saran kepada Dewan Komisaris terkait adanya potensi benturan kepentingan Perseroan.  
14. Menjaga kerahasiaan dokumen, data, dan informasi Perseroan.  
15. Melaksanakan tugas lain dari Dewan Komisaris terkait dengan peran dan tanggung jawab Dewan Komisaris.

# Independency

All members of the Audit Committee prioritize their independence, integrity, and objectivity in carrying out their roles, duties, and responsibilities. In addition, the Audit Committee avoids interference and conflicts of interest within the company.

# Duties and Responsibilities

The Audit Committee carries out its duties and responsibilities based on applicable regulations and the Company's Articles of Association, as follows.

1. Reviewing the financial information that will be issued by the Company to the public and/or authorities, including financial reports, projections and other reports related to the Company's financial information, including compliance with accounting standards and policies in the preparation process.  
2. Review compliance with laws and regulations related to the Company's activities.  
3. Provide an independent opinion in the event of a difference of opinion between the management and the external accountant for the services they provide.  
4. Provide recommendations to the Board of Commissioners regarding the appointment of an accountant based on independence, scope of assignment and compensation for services.  
5. Encouraging the establishment of an adequate internal control system in managing the company by evaluating and providing recommendations regarding the improvement of the company's internal control system and its implementation.  
6. Reviewing the implementation of inspections by the internal auditors and overseeing the implementation of follow-up actions by the Board of Directors on the findings of the internal auditors.  
7. Reviewing the implementation of risk management system activities carried out by the Board of Directors.  
8. Examine complaints related to the Company's accounting and financial reporting processes.  
9. Examine the independence and objectivity of public accountants.  
10. Reviewing the adequacy of audits conducted by public accountants.  
11. Examine allegations of errors in the decisions of the Board of Directors meetings or irregularities in implementing the decisions of the Board of Directors meetings.  
12. Delivering the review report to all members of the Company's Board of Commissioners after the completion of the review report conducted by the Audit Committee.  
13. Review and provide advice to the Board of Commissioners regarding potential conflicts of interest of the Company.  
14. Maintain the confidentiality of the Company's documents, data, and information.  
15. Carry out other duties of the Board of Commissioners related to the roles and responsibilities of the Board of Commissioners.

# Pelaksanaan Tugas

Pada tahun 2023, Komite Audit telah melaksanakan tugas dan tanggung jawab dengan baik dan seksuai dengan pedoman kerja yang berlaku, sebagai berikut.

1. Melakukaan penelaahan terhadap Laporan Keuangan Triwulanan dan Tahunan Perseroan yang disampaikan kepada regulator.  
2. Melakukan pengawasan terhadap sistem pengendalian internal dan manajemen risiko.  
3. Melakukan penelaahan terhadap temuan dari Unit Audit Internal dan Manajemen Risiko, ada memantau tindak lanjut rekomendasi atas temuan audit tersebut.  
4. Menyusun dan menyampaikan laporan tersebut kerja dan rekomendasi kepada Komisaris utama.

# Rapat

Komite Audit melaksanan rapat internal paling kurang 1 kali setiap 3 bulan, atas dilaksanan sewaktu-waktu sesuai kepentingan ketua komite ataupun Dewan Komisaris. Sepanjang tahun 2023, Komite Audit telah melaksanan rapat sebanyak 7 kali, yang diuraikan sebagai berikut.

# Implementation of Duties

In 2023, the Audit Committee has carried out its duties and responsibilities properly and in accordance with applicable work guidelines, as follows.

1. Conduct a review of the Company's Quarterly and Annual Financial Statements submitted to the regulator.  
2. Supervise the internal control system and risk management.  
3. Review the findings of the Internal Audit and Risk Management Unit, and monitor the follow-up of recommendations on the audit findings.  
4. Prepare and submit reports on work results and recommendations to the President Commissioner.

# Meeting

The Audit Committee conducts internal meetings at least 1 time every 3 months, or is held at any time according to the interests of the chairman of the committee or the Board of Commissioners. Throughout 2023, the Audit Committee has held as many meetings as 7 times, which are outlined as follows.

Komite Audit melaksanakan kegiatan pengembangan kompetensi dalam upaya memperlugas pemaham dan wawasan terkait aktivitas bisnis yang difalankan dan memaksimalkan pelaksanaan tugas. Sepanjang tahun 2023, Komite Audit telah mengikuti kegiatan pengembangan kompetensi sebagai berikut.

# KOMITE NOMINASI DAN REMUNERASI

# NOMINATION AND REMUNERATION COMMITTEE

Komite Nominasi dan Remunerasi tersebut komitedi bawah Dewan Komisaris yang dibentuk untukmelaksanan kebujakan nominasi dan remunerasi bagiDewan Komisaris, Direksi, dan kanyakan Perseroan.

# Pedoman Kerja

Komite Nominasi dan Remunerasi melaksanakan tugas dan tanggung jawabnya berdasarkan Peraturan Otoritas Jasa Keuangan No. 34/POJK.04/2014 tersebut Komite Nominasi dan Remunerasi Emiten atas Perusahaan Publik.

# Komposisi dan Keanggotaan

Pada tahun 2023, komposisi dan keanggotaan Komite Nominasi dan Remunerasi Perseroan terdiri dari 1 Ketua yang dibjabat oleh Komisaris Independen, serta 2 orang anggota yang bersal dari anggota Dewan Komisaris dan pihak Perseroan yang menjadi di bidang sumber daya manusia (SDM), yang diuraikan sebagai berikut.

The Nomination and Remuneration Committee is a committee under the Board of Commissioners established to implement nomination and remuneration policies for the Board of Commissioners, Board of Directors, and employees of the Company.

# Work Guidelines

The Nomination and Remuneration Committee carries out its duties and responsibilities based on the Financial Services Authority Regulation No. 34/POJK.04/2014 concerning the Nomination and Remuneration Committee of Issuers or Public Companies.

# Composition and Membership

In 2023, the composition and membership of the Company's Nomination and Remuneration Committee consists of 1 Chairman held by an Independent Commissioner, and 2 members from members of the Board of Commissioners and the Company serving in the field of human resources (HR), which are described as follows.

# Independensi

Seluruh anggota Komite Nominasi dan Remunerasi mengutamakan independensinya, integritas, dan objektivitas dalam melaksanakan peran, tugas, serta tanggung jawabnya. Selain itu, komite ini menghindari adanya intervensi dan benturan kepentingan di internal perusahaan.

# Tugas dan Tanggung Jawab

Komite Nominasi dan Remunerasi menjalankan tugas dan tanggung jawab, sebagai berikut.

1. Memberikan rekomendasi kepada Dewan Komisaris mengenai:

a. Komposisi jabatan anggota Direksi dan/atau anggota Dewan Komisaris;  
b. Kebijakan dan kriteria yang dibutuhkan dalam proses nominasi; dan  
c. Kebijakan evaluasi kinerja bagi anggota Direksi dan/ atau anggota Dewan Komisaris.

2. Membantu Dewan Komisarispekukanan penilaian kinerja anggota Direksi dan/atau anggota Dewan Komisaris berdasarkan untuk ukur yang telah disusun sebagai bahan evaluasi.  
3. Memberikan rekomendasi mengenai program pengembangan kemampuan anggota Direksi dan/atau anggota Dewan Komisaris.  
4. Menyusun dan memberikan rekomendasi mengenai systemd serta prosedur pemilihan dan/atau penggantian anggota Direksi dan/atau Dewan Komisaris kepada Dewan Komisaris.  
5. Memberikan usulan calon yang memenuhi syarat minimal sebagai mania ditentukan oleh Otoritas Jasa Keuangan sebagai anggota Direksi dan/atau anggota Dewan Komisaris untuk disampaikan kepada RUPS.  
6. Memberikan rekomendasi mengai pihak independen yang akan menjadi anggota Komite Audit atau Komite lainnya kepada Dewan Komisaris.  
7. Melakukan evaluasi terhadap kebijakan remunerasi yang didasarkan atas kinerja, risiko, kewajaran dengan peer group, sasan dan strategi jangka panjang Perseroan, pemenuhan cadangan sebagai diatur dalam peraturan perdang-undangan dan potensi pendapatan Perseroan di masa yang akan datang.  
8. Menyampaikan研究成果

b. Kebijakan remunerasi bagi pegawai secara keseluruhan untuk disampaikan kepada Direksi.

9. Memastikan telah kebujakan remunerasi telah sesuai dengan ketentuan yang berlaku.  
10. Melakukan evaluasi secara Berkala terhadap pengerapan kebjikan remunerasi.  
11. Memberikan rekomendasi(OPengai:

a. Struktur remunerasi;  
b. Kebijakan atas remunerasi; dan

c. Besaran atas remunerasi.

12. Membantu Dewan Komisarispekukanan penilaian kinerja dengankesesuaian remunerasi yang diterima masing-masing anggota Direksi dan/atau anggota Dewan Komisaris.

# Independence

All members of the Nomination and Remuneration Committee prioritize their independence, integrity, and objectivity in carrying out their roles, duties, and responsibilities. In addition, this committee avoids interference and conflicts of interest within the company.

# Duties and Responsibilities

The Nomination and Remuneration Committee carries out its duties and responsibilities, as follows.

1. Provide recommendations to the Board of Commissioners regarding:

a. Position composition of members of the Board of Directors and/or members of the Board of Commissioners;  
b. Policies and criteria needed in the nomination process; and  
c. Performance evaluation policy for members of the Board of Directors and/or members of the Board of Commissioners.

2. Assist the Board of Commissioners in evaluating the performance of members of the Board of Directors and/or members of the Board of Commissioners based on benchmarks that have been prepared as evaluation material.  
3. Provide recommendations regarding capacity building programs for members of the Board of Directors and/or members of the Board of Commissioners.  
4. Prepare and provide recommendations regarding the system and procedure for selecting and/or replacing members of the Board of Directors and/or Board of Commissioners to the Board of Commissioners.  
5. Provide proposals for candidates who meet the minimum requirements as determined by Financial Services Authority as members of the Board of Directors and/or members of the Board of Commissioners to be submitted to the GMS.  
6. Provide recommendations regarding independent parties who will become members of the Audit Committee or other Committees to the Board of Commissioners.  
7. Evaluate the remuneration policy based on performance, risk, fairness with the peer group, the Company's long-term goals and strategies, fulfillment of reserves as stipulated in the laws and regulations and the Company's future income potential.  
8. Deliver evaluation results and recommendations to the Board of Commissioners regarding:

a. Remuneration policy for the Board of Directors and Board of Commissioners to be submitted to the GMS; and  
b. Remuneration policy for employees as a whole to be submitted to the Board of Directors.

9. Ensuring that the remuneration policy complies with the applicable regulations.  
10. Periodically evaluate the implementation of the remuneration policy.  
11. Provide recommendations regarding:

a. remuneration structure;  
b. Policy on remuneration; and  
c. Amount of remuneration.

12. Assist the Board of Commissioners in evaluating performance according to the suitability of the remuneration received by each member of the Board of Directors and/or members of the Board of Commissioners.

# Pelaksanaan Tugas

Sepanjang tahun 2023, Komite Nominasi dan Remunerasi telah melaksanan tugas dan tanggung jawab kerkit kebujakan remunerasi bagi Dewan Komisaris, Direksi,serta karyawan Perseroan.

# Rapat

Rapat internal Komite Nominasi dan Remunerasi dilaksanan paling kurang 1 kali dalam 3 bulan. Pada tahun 2023, komite ini telah melaksananRAPAT sebanyak 4 kali, dengan tingkat kehadiran sebagai berikut.

# Implementation of Duties

Throughout 2023, the Nomination and Remuneration Committee has carried out duties and responsibilities related to remuneration policy for the Board of Commissioners, Board of Directors, and employees of the Company.

# Meeting

Internal meetings of the Nomination and Remuneration Committee are held at least 1 time in 3 months. In 2023, this committee has held as many meetings as 4 times, with attendance rates as follows.

# SEKRETARIS PERUSAHAAN

# CORPORATE SECRETARY

Sekretaris Perusahaan merupakan organ pendukung Direksi yang membantu untuk mengatur dan mengelola komunikasi antara Perseroan dengan Pemegang Saham dan pemangku kepada pengentingan lainnya. Selain itu, Sekretaris Perusahaan bertanggung jawab untuk说我mpaikan laporan-laporan kepada regulator secara的前提下 menata dengan rapi dokumen dan proses administrasi perusahaan.

# Pedoman Kerja

Sekretaris Perusahaan menjalankan tugas dan tanggung jawab berpedoman pada Peraturan Otoritas Jasa Keuangan No. 35/POJK.04/2014tentang Sekretaris Perusahaan Emiten atop Perusahaan Publik.

# Profil Sekretaris Perusahaan

Sekretaris Perusahaanunjiahobeluyosuseno yangnya merupakan Direktur Perseroan.Beliaudiangkat berdasarkan Surat Keputusan Direksi PT Pelita Teknologi Global Tbk No.001/SKD-CS/X/PTG/2022 tanggal 10 Oktober 2022tentang Pengangkatan Sekretaris Perusahaan PT Pelita Teknologi Global Tbk.Informasi terkait profil Sekretaris Perusahaan tetlah disampaikan pada Bab Profil Perusahaan di dalam Laporan Tahunan ini.

# Tugas dan Tanggung Jawab

Sekretaris Perusahaan menjalankan tugas dan tanggung jawab sebagai berikut.

1. Mengikuti perkembangan相对较 modal khususnya peraturan-peraturan yang berlaku di bidang相对较 modal.  
2. Memberikan masukan kepada Direksi dan Dewan Komisaris Perseroan untuk mematuhi ketentuan peraturan perdang-undangan di bidang相伴 modal.  
3. Membantu Direksi dan Dewan Komisaris dalam pelaksanaan tata kelola Perseroan yang meliputi:

a. Keterbukaan informasi kepada masyarakat, termasuk ketersediaan informasi pada situs web Perseroan;  
b. Penyampaian laporan kepada Otoritas Jasa Keuangan tersebut waktu;  
c. Penyelenggaraan dan dokumentasi RUPS;  
d. Penyelenggaraan dan dokumentasi rapat Direksi dan/atau Dewan Komisaris; serta  
e. Pelaksanaan program orientasi terhadap Perseroan bagi Direksi dan/atau Dewan Komisaris.

4. Sebagai penghubung antara Perseroan dengan Pemegang Saham Perseroan, Otoritas Jasa Keuangan, dan pemangku kepentingan lainnya.

The Corporate Secretary is a supporting organ of the Board of Directors that helps to regulate and manage communication between the Company and Shareholders and other stakeholders. In addition, the Corporate Secretary is responsible for submitting reports to regulators in a timely manner and neatly organizing the company's administrative documents and processes.

# Work Guidelines

The Corporate Secretary carries out duties and responsibilities based on the Financial Services Authority Regulation No. 35/POJK.04/2014 concerning Corporate Secretary of Issuers or Public Companies.

# Corporate Secretary Profile

The Corporate Secretary is held by Mulyo Suseno who is also the Director of the Company. He was appointed based on the Decree of the Board of Directors of PT Pelita Teknologi Global Tbk No. 001/SKD-CS/X/PTG/2022 dated October 10, 2022 concerning the Appointment of Corporate Secretary of PT Pelita Teknologi Global Tbk. Information related to the profile of the Corporate Secretary has been submitted in the Company Profile Chapter in this Annual Report.

# Duties and Responsibilities

The Corporate Secretary carries out the following duties and responsibilities.

1. Keep abreast of Capital Market developments, especially regulations applicable in the capital market sector.  
2. Provide input to the Directors and Board of Commissioners of the Company to comply with the provisions of laws and regulations in the Capital Market sector.  
3. Assisting the Board of Directors and Board of Commissioners in the implementation of corporate governance which includes:

a. Information disclosure to the public, including the availability of information on the Company's website;  
b. Timely submission of reports to the Financial Services Authority;  
c. Implementation and documentation of the General Meeting of Shareholders;  
d. Organization and documentation of meetings of the Board of Directors and/or the Board of Commissioners; and  
e. Implementation of an orientation program for the Board of Directors and/or the Board of Commissioners of the Company.

4. Act as a liaison between the Company and the Company's shareholders, the Financial Services Authority, and other stakeholders.

# Pelaksanaan Tugas

Sekretaris Perusaan telah seksukanan peran, tugas dan tanggung jawab seksuai dengan pedoman kerja yang berlaku, serta telah efektif diterapkan seksuai dengan pelaksanaan tugasnya, yang diuraikan sebagai berikut.

1. Menyelenggaraman RUPS Tahunan dan Paparan Publik pada tanggal 20 Juni 2023.  
2. Menyusun dan melaporkan laporan-laporan berkala kepada regulator.  
3. Mendokumentasikan rapat internal Direksi, rapat gabungan Dewan Komisaris dan Direksi,{serta rapatrapat bersama komite/organ lainnya.  
4. Memperbarui informasi di situs web perusaan dan situs web Bursa Efek Indonesia secaraBERkala.

# Pengembangan Kompetensi

Sekretaris Perusahaan melaksakan kegiatan pengembangan kompetensi dalam upaya memperlugas pemahaman dan wawasan terkait aktivitas bisnis yang difalankan dan memaksimalkan pelaksanaan tugas. Sepanjang tahun 2023, Sekretaris Perusahaan telah mengikuti kegiatan pengembangan kompetensi sebagai berikut.

# Implementation of Duties

The Corporate Secretary has performed roles, duties and responsibilities in accordance with applicable work guidelines, and has been effectively implemented in accordance with the implementation of his duties, which are described as follows.

1. Holding the Annual GMS and Public Expose on June 20, 2023.  
2. Prepare and report periodic reports to regulators.  
3. Document internal meetings of the Board of Directors, joint meetings of the Board of Commissioners and Board of Directors, and joint meetings of other committees/organs.  
4. Update the information on the company's website and Indonesia Stock Exchange website regularly.

# Competency Development

The Corporate Secretary carries out competency development activities in an effort to broaden understanding and insight related to business activities carried out and maximize the implementation of duties. Throughout 2023, the Corporate Secretary has participated in the following competency development activities.

# UNIT AUDIT INTERNAL

# INTERNAL AUDIT UNIT

Direksi membrantuk organ pendukung, yaitu Unit Audit Internal yang berfungsi untuk membuat proses kerja di internal Perseroan, membantu Komite Audit dalam aktivakan audit Laporan Keuangan,serta bertanggung jawab dalam;penerapan dan pengawasan;(system pengendalian internal,istem manajemen risiko, dan GCG Perseroan.

# Pedoman Kerja

Unit Audit Internal menjalankan tugas dan tanggung jawab berpedoman pada Piagam Unit Audit Internal yang telah ditetapkan oleh Direksi Perseroan berdasarkan Surat Keputusan No.004/SKD-IAU/X/PTG/2022tentang Pengangkatan dan/atau Pembentukan Unit Audit Internal dan Piagam Unit Audit Internal PT Pelita Teknologi Global Tbk tanggal 10 Oktober 2022 dengan Persetujuan Dewan Komisaris Perseroan. Piagam tersebut telah disesuaikan dengan Peraturan Otoritas Jasa Keuangan No.56/POJK.04/2015 tanggal 23 Desember 2015 inginumbentukan dan Pedoman Penyusunan Piagam Unit Audit Internal.

The Board of Directors establishes a supporting organ, which is the Internal Audit Unit which functions to audit the Company's internal work processes, assist the Audit Committee in auditing the Financial Statements, and is responsible for the implementation and supervision of the Company's internal control system, risk management system, and GCG.

# Work Guidelines

The Internal Audit Unit carries out its duties and responsibilities based on the Internal Audit Unit Charter stipulated by the Company's Board of Directors based on Decree No. 004/SKD-IAU/X/PTG/2022 concerning the Appointment and/or Establishment of the Internal Audit Unit and the Internal Audit Unit Charter of PT Pelita Teknologi Global Tbk on October 10, 2022 with the Approval of the Company's Board of Commissioners. The Charter has been adjusted to the Financial Services Authority Regulation No. 56/POJK.04/2015 on December 23, 2015 concerning the Establishment and Guidelines for the Preparation of the Internal Audit Unit Charter.

Adapun isi dari piagam Unit Audit Internal tersebutteringkait fungsi dan ruang lingkup Satuan Kerja Audit Internal dalam memberikan jasa assurance dan consulting yang independen dan obyektif guna memberikan nilai tambah dan perbaikan terhadap operasional Perseroan. Selain itu, Unit Audit Internal membrantu Perseroan dalam mencapai tujuannya melalui penggunaan metode yang sistematis dalam mengevaluasi dan mencatkan efektivitas risk management, internal control, dan governance process.

# Profil Unit Audit Internal

Pada tahun 2023, Kepala Unit Audit Internal bijat oleh Rama Firmansyah Poetra, dengan uraian profil beliau diungkapkan sebagai berikut.

The contents of the Internal Audit Unit charter are related to the function and scope of the Internal Audit Work Unit in providing independent and objective assurance and consulting services in order to provide added value and improvements to the Company's operations. In addition, the Internal Audit Unit assists the Company in achieving its objectives through the use of systematic methods in evaluating and improving the effectiveness of risk management, internal control, and governance processes.

# Internal Audit Unit Profile

In 2023, the Head of Internal Audit Unit will be Rama Firmansyah Poetra, with his profile description revealed as follows.

# Struktur dan Kedudukan

Unit Audit Internal secara langsung bertanggung jawab kepada Direktur Utama,{serta mempunyai hak dan wewenang untuk Berkomunikasi dengan Dewan Komisaris ataupun seluruh pihak di dalam Perseroan dalam pelaksanaan tugas dan tanggung jawabnya. Selain itu, Unit Audit Internal mempunyai wewenang untuk bekerja sama dengan Komite Audit ataupun Auditor Eksternal dalam menganalisa telah audit, terutama tersebut Laporan Keuangan Perseroan.

# Structure and Position

The Internal Audit Unit is directly responsible to the President Director, and has the right and authority to communicate with the Board of Commissioners or all parties in the Company in carrying out its duties and responsibilities. In addition, the Internal Audit Unit has the authority to cooperate with the Audit Committee or External Auditor in analyzing audit results, especially related to the Company's Financial Statements.

# Tugas dan Tanggung Jawab

Tugas dan tanggung jawab yang difalankan oleh Unit Audit Internal diuraikan sebagai berikut.

1. Menyusun dan melaksanakan rencana audit internal tahunan.  
2. Menguji dan mangevaluasi pelaksanaan pengendalian internal dan systemd manajemen risiko seksui dengan kebikan Perseroan.  
3. Melakukan pemeriksaan dan penilaian atas efisiensi dan efektivitas di bidang keuangan, akuntansi, operasional, sumber daya manusia, pemasaran, tekologi informasi dan kegiatan lainnya.  
4. Memberikan saran perbaikan dan informasi yang objektif ingin terang kegiatan yang diperiksa pada semua tingkat manajemen.  
5. Membuat laporan tersebut audit dan mencyampaikan laporan tersebut kepada Direktur Utama dan Dewan Komisaris.  
6. Memantau, menganalisis dan melaporkan pelaksanaan tindak lanjut perbaikan yang telah disarankan.  
7. Bekerja sama dengan Komite Audit.  
8. Menyusun program untuk mengevaluasi kutu kegiatan audit internal yang dilakukanya.  
9. Melakukan pemeriksaan khusus apabila diperlukan.

# Wewenang

1. Mengakses seluruh informasi yang relevanttentang Perseroan terkait dengan tugas dan fungsinya.  
2. Melakukan komunikasi secara langsung dengan Direksi, Dewan Komisaris, dan/atau Komite Audituminiuma anggota dari Direksi, Dewan Komisaris, dan/atau Komite Audit.  
3. Mengadakan rapat secara bergala dan insidencil Dengan Direksi, Dewan Komisaris, dan/atau Komite Audit.  
4. Melakukan koordinasi kegiatannya dengan kegiatan auditor eksternal.

# Pelaksanaan Tugas

Pada tahun 2023, Unit Audit Internal telah melaksanakan tugas dan tanggung jawabnya dengan baik dan efektif,(SEbagai berikut.

1. Menerapkan dan mengawasi;penerapan systemd pengendalian internal dan manajemen risiko,erta memberikan assurance terhadap;penerapan tersebut kepada Dewan Komisaris dan Direksi.  
2. Melakukan pengawasan terhadap aktivitas operasional, aktivitas keuangan, dan;penerapan GCG yang berkoordinasi dengan Komite Audit.  
3. Menyampaikan laporan bulanan dan tahun terkait pelaksanaan tugas audit internal kepada Direksi melalui rapat gabungan.

# Duties and Responsibilities

The duties and responsibilities carried out by the Internal Audit Unit are described as follows.

1. Prepare and implement an annual internal audit plan.  
2. Test and evaluate the implementation of internal control and risk management systems in accordance with Company policies.  
3. Examine and evaluate efficiency and effectiveness in finance, accounting, operations, human resources, marketing, information technology and other activities.  
4. Provide suggestions for improvement and objective information about the activities examined at all levels of management.  
5. Make a report on the results of the audit and submit the report to the President Director and the Board of Commissioners.  
6. Monitor, analyze and report on the implementation of follow-up improvements that have been suggested.  
7. Cooperate with the Audit Committee.  
8. Formulate a program to evaluate the quality of the internal audit activities it performs.  
9. Carry out special inspections if necessary.

# Authorities

1. Access all relevant information about the Company related to its duties and functions.  
2. Communicating directly with the Board of Directors, Board of Commissioners and/or the Audit Committee and members of the Board of Directors, Board of Commissioners and/or the Audit Committee.  
3. Hold regular and incidental meetings with the Board of Directors, Board of Commissioners and/or the Audit Committee.  
4. Coordinate its activities with the activities of the external auditors.

# Implementation of Duties

In 2023, the Internal Audit Unit has carried out its duties and responsibilities properly and effectively, as follows.

1. Implement and supervise the implementation of internal control and risk management systems, as well as provide assurance on the implementation to the Board of Commissioners and Board of Directors.  
2. Supervise operational activities, financial activities, and GCG implementation in coordination with the Audit Committee.  
3. Submit monthly and annual reports related to the implementation of internal audit duties to the Board of Directors through joint meetings.

# Rapat Unit Audit Internal

Kepala Unit Audit Internal tersebut rapat gabungan bersama Dewan Komisaris, Direksi, seda Komite Audit minimal 1 kali dalam setahun. Kepala Unit Audit Internal juga dapat melaksananRAPAT secara insidental sesuai dengan kebutuhan Direksi Perseroan. Sepanjang tahun 2023, Kepala Unit Audit Internal telah tersebut 3 kaliRAPAT terkait Laporan Keuangan Perseroan, seda pengembangan dan;penerapan standar ISO Perseroan.

# Pengembangan Kompetensi

Kepala Unit Audit Internal melaksanan kegiatan pengembangan kompetensi dalam upaya memperluas pemahaman dan wawasan terkait aktivitas bisnis yang difalankan dan memaksimalkan pelaksanaan tugas. Sepanjang tahun 2023, Unit Audit Internal telah mengikut kegiatan pengembangan kompetensi sebagai berikut.

# Internal Audit Unit Meeting

The Head of the Internal Audit Unit attends joint meetings with the Board of Commissioners, Directors and Audit Committee at least once a year. The Head of the Internal Audit Unit can also hold incidental meetings according to the needs of the Company's Board of Directors. Throughout 2023, the Head of the Internal Audit Unit has attended 3 meetings related to the Company's Financial Report, as well as the development and implementation of the Company's ISO standards.

# Competency Development

The Head of Internal Audit Unit carries out competency development activities in an effort to broaden understanding and insight related to business activities carried out and maximize the implementation of tasks. Throughout 2023, the Internal Audit Unit has participated in the following competency development activities.
